We had expected growth to progress by planting them with Evil Weeds, but they’ve become considerably larger than normal… The remaining question is the taste.

I just hope they don’t turn out bland. I wonder how they’ll be.

+++

# **329 – Tasting Event of the Giant Pumpkin**

“Hmm… Seeing them again, they’ve really grown quite a bit.”

The next day—today was a rest day from Knight Order training. Since letting the pumpkins grow any larger would be problematic, I went to check the field we’d created beside the storage shed, where several Monster Pumpkins were sitting majestically on the straw.

The pumpkins’ condition—thanks to everyone’s diligent care, they had colored beautifully and gave the impression that now was the perfect harvest time.

As for the Evil Weeds, they were peeking their faces out between the straw and pumpkins, basking comfortably in the sunlight.

“I thought turning them over would be difficult since they grew so large, but with the magic tools, maintenance was easy,” said Cyrille the Centaur with a smile.

“I’m glad the magic tools were useful.”

When pumpkins approach harvest time, you need to turn them to change which side gets sunlight… but with the Levitation Magic Tool, that effort isn’t too burdensome. It’s a repurposing of aerial combat gear, but it’s what you’d call effective utilization.

The Evil Weeds are merely agricultural supplements. To make crops bear fruit well, human hands are still necessary.

“With this many, cooking them all seems like it’ll be tough.”

“I don’t think we need to eat them all after harvesting. Assuming they taste good, it might be better to take one or two to the Barony of Silun and have them cooked there for tasting.”

“I see. Showing them the actual thing and having them taste it is better than just explanations.”

Rosemary nodded as if convinced.

“We’ve entrusted the Evil Weeds to the old man, and he said crops are growing larger in his fields too.”

“With pumpkins this size, normally the flavor would deteriorate. Showing them together should serve as good evidence.”

“That’s true. We’re incorporating Evil Weeds into farming methods, and having actual harvests makes the credibility different.”

I nodded at Ashley and Claudia’s words.

So we all started harvesting the pumpkins. Throughout the harvesting, the Evil Weeds remained quiet. They didn’t become aggressive or interfere with the harvest.

“Since cold days will increase from now on, it might be better to return the Evil Weeds to pots and bring them indoors at night.”

“I read in a book that they can survive through the year if kept in warm places.”

That resilience makes you remember they’re monsters after all.

Hmm… Then let’s transplant them right away while harvesting. Using Earth Magic and Levitation, I dug up the surrounding soil and returned them to pots without damaging their roots.

After finishing the harvest, we decided to let the pumpkins rest for a few days, then divide the work among us to make pumpkin dishes.

With this quantity, it seemed today would be all about pumpkins—not just the originally planned pumpkin pies, but also soups, cookies, and more… But with the Labyrinth Village residents also present, there wouldn’t be any leftovers.

“Hmm. With them this big, maybe we should use magic to cut the pumpkins too.”

I levitated the Monster Pumpkins brought to the kitchen, washed them with water, then cut them using Water Magic. Then I further divided them into sizes suitable for each dish. The cut surfaces showed nothing unusual—they just looked like regular pumpkins, only larger.

“Then, let’s begin.”

At Mihaela’s words, everyone nodded. For some reason, I felt the female members were particularly motivated.

Camilla had also rolled up her sleeves, excited to serve Elliot some delicious pumpkin dishes.

Mihaela, Cecilia, Grace, and Rosemary took charge of pumpkin pies. Marlene, Sheila, Camilla, and Valentina handled the soup. Ashley, Claudia, Irmhild, Seraphina, and Charlotte were in charge of making sweets.

Claire, Cyrille, Irmhild’s parents, and the Labyrinth Village residents were also divided into groups to make pumpkin dishes together.

Elliot, Old Sigmund, and I took on supporting roles like cutting ingredients and mashing pumpkins. Elliot was quite skilled with a knife too.

“Elliot-san, you seem quite accustomed to cooking.”

“During my early days in Silvatoria, there was a period when I cooked for myself,” Elliot said while cutting pumpkins with a laugh.

I see. Before he distinguished himself as a Magic Knight, he must have had various hardships.

Old Sigmund and I divided the steamed, softened pumpkins and used Wind Magic to crush them into paste, actively incorporating magic into cooking.

“Hmm. Using magic like this is enjoyable,” Old Sigmund said with a smile.

“Making magic serve daily life… that’s the philosophy of Tower magicians.”

“That’s right. It’s slightly different from the Sages’ Academy’s purpose.”

Charlotte and Valentina exchanged words while cooking.

As we cooked harmoniously together, the sweet aroma of pies and cookies being made stimulated our nostrils. I was looking forward to the results.

With many hands making light work, I had some free time, so I decided to make one simple dish myself.

Removing the seeds, I cut the pumpkin into bite-sized pieces and put them in a pot. Covering it, I used Wind Magic and Water Magic to pressurize and heat it. Once softened enough for a skewer to pass through, I transferred it to a dish, added chopped bacon, lightly sprinkled salt and spices, then topped it with cheese—finally lightly roasting it with Fire Magic. Pumpkin cheese bake. Being a simple dish, it was finished in no time.

“That looks delicious,” Sheila said, looking at the finished dish.

Apparently, using magic for cooking had drawn everyone’s attention. Well, partly because the ovens were occupied, so I used magic.

“Well, as a snack substitute.”

So we all decided to have a light taste. This would be an important item for gauging the results of Evil Weed farming methods. First, I tried it myself.

Hmm… When it enters my mouth, the flavor of roasted cheese, the pumpkin’s aroma, and sweetness spread throughout.

Hmm. Similar to the water quality of the Fire Spirit Hot Spring, perhaps. Whether I feel magical power is present because I used magic in the cooking process or because it was planted with Evil Weeds…

Curious, I carefully examined an untouched, uncut pumpkin… Yeah. It seems to have contained some magical power from the beginning.

When ingredients contain magical power, it adds depth to the flavor, similar to monster ingredients, perhaps. Unexpectedly, might this be better than regular pumpkins?

“Hmm… Yes. This is good quality.”

“It’s fluffy and delicious.”

“I thought growing too large might affect the pumpkin’s flavor… but that seems to have been unnecessary worry.”

Everyone’s reviews weren’t bad. Since I didn’t do anything particularly elaborate, this must be largely thanks to the Evil Weeds’ contribution. The idea of utilizing Evil Weeds in farming methods seems like it might work out well.

The pies and soup were finished, and the cookies were baked too. The time was just past noon. Quantity-wise, it was plenty. We set up tables in the courtyard, having a tasting party under the blue sky.

“This is… delicious.”

The pie had a flaky crust with just the right sweetness… Yeah. From texture to taste, including visual appeal, it’s exquisite. Worthy of Cecilia’s strong endorsement as Mihaela’s specialty dish, you could say. The soup with basil sprinkled on top is perfectly seasoned too. The baked sweets are crisp and go well with tea. The cooking methods are probably good, but the pumpkin itself must taste good too. I can feel magical power as well. The way the magical power works… still similar to the hot spring’s. Doesn’t seem harmful to the body.

Thinking that an all-pumpkin menu might become tiresome, we also prepared sausages, bacon, and such.

The Labyrinth Village residents, either in high spirits from the cheerful atmosphere or because they were assigned, brought out instruments and started singing and dancing. Seraphina was happily flying around.

“Hmm. Good work,” I said, lightly patting the heads of the Evil Weeds we’d potted and placed in the courtyard. They shook their heads, quivering.

Watching them, Harvesta turned her head around… then quietly placed seeds she held in her mouth at the base of her pot. …Somehow, it looks like she’s entrusting the seeds to us.

“…Is it okay to take the seeds?”

Saying this, I picked up the seeds, but Harvesta didn’t attack. Seeing this, the other Evil Weeds followed suit, as if following the example.

…Would you call this a symbiotic relationship? Perhaps the Evil Weeds have recognized humans as partners. Maybe they’ve learned that being under human protection means safety?

Anyway, I’ll gratefully take care of the seeds. I was wondering whether the changes in Evil Weeds’ nature would continue or be limited to one generation, and how to handle seed collection. This is a welcome development.

For Elliot and Camilla’s wedding, we’ve invited Father and Malcolm too. Naturally, we’ll discuss the Evil Weeds with both of them then. This will surely be useful not just for the barony but also for developing farmland in the Marquisate of Broderick.

+++

# **330 – Sirius Ascending**

“Well then, let’s begin the next one.”

“Whenever you’re ready.”

Sitting in the center of the Magic Array drawn in a room of the shipyard facility, Irmhild took a deep breath.

In her hand was a Magic Stone extracted from a Lesser Demon. As Valentina deployed her Magic Circle, the Magic Array glowed in response, and the Magic Stone in Irmhild’s hand began to shine with a bright purple light.

“Mmm, mmm, hmm-hmm~”

Seraphina sat perched on my shoulder, humming a tune. It was the same song Irmhild had played before. She swung her legs back and forth, looking quite cheerful, but she wasn’t just playing around… She was currently projecting sound straight forward over a long distance. She was using humming as a means to continuously produce sound.

While sensing the flow of Magical Power through Circulating Ki and converting it into a Spell Formula, I was preparing various patterns—diffusing it, focusing it, and so on.

Looking at the paper with the written Spell Formula, Alfred nodded.

“Yeah. I think this is sufficient for sound manipulation.”

“Thank you, Seraphina.”

“No problem. It was fun.”

Seraphina smiled, then left my shoulder and began flying around the room.

“Well then, shall we make Seraphina-chan’s Magic Stone next?”

“Mm-hmm!”

Called by Valentina, Seraphina flew over carrying her Magic Stone.

“Then, next is my Cursed Melody, I suppose?”

Irmhild said, holding her Lute.

“That’s right. I’ll observe the flow of Magical Power while you play the Cursed Melody and perform Circulating Ki.”

“Okay. Leave it to me.”

Irmhild, who had released her Humanization Spell, skillfully twisted her body to pick up her Lute and came over to me.

“Well then, please take care of me, Theodore-kun.”

“Understood.”

Once again, just like before, I was lightly wrapped by Irmhild’s tail. It had a somewhat smooth texture. It’s true that the more surface area we’re in contact with, the easier it is to sense the flow of Magical Power.

As I began Circulating Ki, Irmhild started playing her Cursed Melody with a somewhat cheerful air. I closed my eyes, sensing the movement of Magical Power, and wrote it down on paper.

Whether it was Irmhild’s music or Seraphina’s humming… the atmosphere was so peaceful it was hard to believe we were developing a Sonic Cannon.

Well then. Once I finished writing the Spell Formula, it was time to continue with the airship’s interior work.

“How about decorations in this style around here…?”

“I think that’s good. It looks quite dignified too.”

Rosemary nodded quietly.

We spread out books on architecture and consulted with everyone while building the interior of the Sirius. We used Wood Magic to process Wood and assemble the internal structure, then added fine decorations as interior finishing to the completed parts. In terms of the process, we were probably close to the final stages.

“With the interior coming together, it really starts to look the part.”

Ashley smiled as she looked at the results, and Marlene gently touched the completed decoration—the relief portion of the wall.

“The Sonic Cannon still needs a bit more work, but it’s not necessary for the wedding.”

Claudia smiled brightly. As for the trip to the Barony of Silun, conducting a flight test should resolve any issues. The construction of the airship, which we had been progressing alongside preparations for Elliot’s wedding and training for the Demon-Slaying Knight Order, was reaching its climax.

The internal structure of the Sirius, excluding the bridge, consisted of four Floors. At the very bottom, attached to the keel section of the hull, were three Silvatoria-made Levitation Furnaces.

The Magic Stone from the Werewolf progenitor, which served as the power source, was placed directly below the bridge, at the center of the ship.

The four large Magic Stones from the Basilisk, Cockatrice, and others were positioned around the Werewolf progenitor’s Magic Stone, with Spell Formulas engraved and linked to it.

Extending circuits from the center as a base point, we built up the internal structure throughout the entire ship. Functions for navigation and external monitors were also concentrated in the bridge directly above. Voice pipes extended from the bridge, allowing verbal communication with various locations.

Inside the hull were corridors, cabins, a kitchen, toilets and baths, cargo holds, living spaces for Wyverns and Earth Dragons, and so on… Since the usable space was limited, we experimented like solving a Puzzle, prioritizing functionality while ensuring habitability as much as possible.

Well, since we anticipated three-dimensional maneuvers, it was unavoidable that chairs, tables, beds, etc., were fixed integrally with the floors and walls.

We moved to the bridge while finishing the interior work in various parts of the ship. The interior of the bridge was spacious. A large round table. It was set up so that strategy meetings and sortie preparations could also be conducted here. Several voice pipes protruded from the left and right walls.

The rear was raised one step; climbing a short staircase led to the area for navigation and external monitoring. Around the navigation seat, Old Sigmund and the others were inspecting the Crystal Panels.

“Good work. How about this area?”

“Hmm. I find it quite easy to see. Almost all the pillars are visible… With practice in navigation, wouldn’t it be possible to perform feats like passing through tight spots right next to the hull?”

“I’d rather not do anything too risky, though.”

I gave a wry smile at Old Sigmund’s words.

The Crystal Panel monitors displayed pillars erected here and there in the shipyard’s plaza. We had grown pillars around the ship at varying heights and distances and were currently checking which areas were visible and which weren’t from inside the ship.

The number of Crystal Panels in the bridge was twelve in total—front, back, left, right, up, and down. They were positioned three-dimensionally in intuitively understandable locations, allowing a view of all of them from the navigation seat. I wanted someone other than myself to see them and get an objective opinion… but it seemed to leave a good impression.

“Well then… shall we try moving it a bit?”

We had conducted some operational checks after incorporating the core and Magic Stone rooms, but… well, this would be the first flight test after packing various things inside.

“So it’s finally time…”

“Everyone, please disembark and move away for now. As the design lead, I’ll verify the safety.”

“Theo, be careful.”

Grace looked somewhat worried. Well, everyone else did too.

“It’s fine. I’m just going to fly around a bit.”

I said that and returned a smile.

We were just going to fly around the shipyard area. At times like this, having Termwills facing the sea is wonderful—or rather, it’s an environment that makes experiments easy. If anything goes wrong, the area below is the sea, so there would be no damage to the surroundings, and if it’s just me, I can protect myself no matter how many times I crash.

“Well then, let’s move it.”

I contacted everyone outside the ship using the external voice pipe. As everyone watched with bated breath, I hovered my hand over the navigation crystal orb. It was a crystal orb linked to the core Magic Stone.

Following my instructions, the hull began to ascend vertically. I could see the scenery on the external monitors moving slowly vertically as well.

Because we were using large Magic Stones, it was possible to issue all commands from a single crystal orb. Slowly, we traversed the shipyard’s plaza, crossed the outer wall, and looked out over the sea.

Moving forward at low speed. The mechanism that took in wind from the front and directed it backward engaged, gradually increasing our speed.

Looking down at the sea and confirming there were no ships below, I attempted turns, ascents, and descents. The airship tilted gently, turning left and right.

Once we gained speed, I stopped the three Levitation Furnaces and obtained lift via the main wings.

Propulsion was generated by a Magic Tool that directed wind backward, and the shape of the main wings generated lift from the created propulsion.

We weren’t even using the Magic Tools already incorporated into the main wings. This was energy-efficient flight, minimizing Magical Power consumption by using only the tool that took in wind from the front and expelled it backward. It wasn’t full speed yet, but it was quite a nimble pace.

Slowing down, I hovered stationary in the air using only the main wings’ Magic Tools. Adjusting lift from the upper and lower parts of the main wings, I conducted ascent and descent tests.

Next, I operated only the Levitation Furnaces. Combining the output balance of the three with forward propulsion, I performed turns left and right, ascents and descents. Yeah. It moves as I thought it would. The maneuverability isn’t bad. As long as I don’t attempt reckless maneuvers, the interior is quite stable.

‘Any abnormalities seen from outside?’

I contacted everyone via the Communication Device. They replied that there were no problems.

“Now then…”

Well then… the real thing starts from here. I increased speed and moved forward.

“Let’s go, Sirius.”

I touched the crystal orb and issued commands. Through the crystal orb, I sensed some strange Magical Power reaction. This Magical Power… is it from the Werewolf progenitor? Somehow, it felt like that golden wolf was rejoicing—…

The premonition, or rather, an indescribable sensation, lasted only a moment. The fire Magic Tool ignited the massive amount of air being taken in from the front. A blast of wind erupted from the stern. As we accelerated, pressure from the front pressed against my body. The scenery began flowing backward at an incomparably faster speed than before.

High-speed turns, ascents, descents. The armor plates converted the pressure itself exerted on the hull into Magical Power. Consumption was low relative to the speed. Looking outside on the external monitor, I could see a golden shimmer. …I see. That Werewolf progenitor seems to be properly dwelling within the Sirius’s Magic Stone.

After completing the experiments, I slowed down and returned above the shipyard. Carefully, I lowered the ship, stacking it back onto the foundation where it originally rested.

Once the Sirius landed and came to a stop on the ground, something like a golden mist appeared on the round table at the front of the bridge.

“…It’s you.”

The form of a golden wolf on the round table. Not a Werewolf, but a quadrupedal wolf. Should I call it an Ethereal Body? It was hazy, its outline unclear, but when our eyes met, it seemed to grin. It looked away from me, faced forward, and its form vanished.

My impression is… that thing is indeed close to a Spirit.

But I didn’t get a bad impression from it. There’s no doubt it’s cooperating with us.

Although there were some slightly unexpected aspects, the flight test was generally a success, I’d say. At any rate, it seems preparations for heading to the Barony of Silun are complete.

+++

# **331 – To the Barony of Baron Silun**

“Hmm… It’s a beautiful ship, isn’t it?”

For the unveiling of what could be considered the airship’s initial completion, King Melvin came to the shipyard’s plaza and looked up at the Sirius with narrowed eyes.

Those who came to see the Sirius weren’t limited to just King Melvin – Prince Josiah, Princess Stephania, and Princess Adriana were also present. Their escort knights were with them too. Alfred… for some reason was still in disguise and had joined us on the guiding side, but I wondered if that was really appropriate.

“This is wonderful… I heard the ship’s hull itself is made of a special material.”

“Yes. It absorbs impact and converts it into magical power.”

“Oh?”

Prince Josiah’s eyes widened at Princess Stephania’s words, spoken with a cheerful smile, and he lightly knocked on the Sirius’s hull. A faint ripple of light spread along the hull from that point before disappearing. The reason it faded midway was—the impact was too weak, dissipating as it propagated.

“This is fascinating. It looks beautiful too.”

“It’s technology brought from Silvatoria.”

“…I see. As expected of a great magical nation.”

“You honor us. It’s the fruit of the Sages’ Academy’s research. However, creating a hull of this scale was only possible thanks to the ambassador’s power.”

Princess Adriana smiled.

“Thank you.”

We climbed to the deck using the gangplank. A line ran from the bow along the edge of the deck toward the stern in golden paint… giving it quite a magnificent finish. The deck was made of darker-toned wood, creating a relatively calm atmosphere overall.

We could enter the ship’s interior through the door attached to the bridge. Though the door made it appear the hull was segmented… spring-like components extended from locations that wouldn’t obstruct passage and connected to the wall inside, making the entire door essentially one component.

Even if the door were attacked, the damage would be absorbed throughout via the springs, meaning its defense power was ultimately no different from other parts.

We proceeded through the passageway, climbed the stairs, and reached the bridge. Going downward would also allow us to descend into the ship’s interior.

“It’s surprisingly spacious, hardly like being inside a ship.”

“The bridge might be that way. Since we didn’t need sails, we could use the space more generously. The lower areas are somewhat narrower.”

I sat in the pilot’s seat, held my hand over the crystal ball, and started the ship. The scenery outside was projected onto the crystal panels.

The crystal panels arranged in a U-shape along the bridge’s front wall also displayed the outside scenery in a panoramic view. While inside the bridge, one could see a landscape not much different from being on the deck.

“Oh… This is…”

“So we can see the surrounding situation while remaining here?”

“Yes. Now I’ll make us ascend, so please take seats where you can see the pilot’s station. The chairs themselves have belts to prevent you from being thrown out if the ship rocks.”

“How thorough.”

Princess Stephania secured herself to the chair with the seatbelt.

For this unveiling, it was decided we’d take King Melvin and the others for a short flight around Termwills. The Party Members, Alfred, Old Sigmund and his group were sitting around a round table in a slightly lower area, looking relaxed.

The royal members sat in the voice transmission seats behind me, and once everyone had fastened their seatbelts, we ascended vertically. This part went according to the flight tests.

“All piloting is done through this crystal ball. It’s connected to the magic stone room directly below the bridge, and the magic tools move the ship according to the spell formulas engraved on the magic stones. You can’t pilot without understanding the magic tools embedded throughout for propulsion, but once you learn what’s where and how they function, the actual piloting isn’t that difficult, I think.”

While explaining, I advanced the Sirius toward the sea. As the Sirius moved, the scenery flowed past. From Kagehisa’s memories, I’m accustomed to this game-like, indirect field of view—but for everyone else, it must feel fresh.

“Let’s fly along the coastline a bit.”

Saying this, I continued forward. Observing their reactions, without exception, everyone was staring intently at the crystal panels. Grace, Ashley, and Irmhild were smiling happily, while Marlene had shining eyes together with Seraphina. Charlotte was similarly engaged.

Claudia and Rosemary watched with serious, interested expressions. Sheila appeared mostly unchanged at first glance—but her tail was standing straight up, betraying her emotions.

King Melvin and Alfred wore mischievous smiles, while Prince Josiah kept nodding appreciatively. Princess Stephania and Princess Adriana were… getting excited, saying they could see Ceorem through the monitor.

When I sent instructions to the crystal ball, the telescopic function activated on one crystal panel, enlarging Ceorem.

“…So you can zoom in to see things. Amazing,” said Princess Stephania.

Old Sigmund and Valentina narrowed their eyes, and Elliot also looked impressed with his chin in his hand.

Everyone’s reactions were generally favorable. That was what mattered most.

“What are these tube-like things behind us? It says ‘Portside Forward Passageway’…”

“They’re voice pipes. They connect to various parts of the ship, allowing direct verbal communication by speaking into them.”

“No need for messengers, then.”

“Everything is centralized here… truly functional,” remarked King Melvin and Prince Josiah.

“I thought it would rock more, but it’s quiet.”

“That’s true when flying straight. But sharp turns and rapid ascents/descents will likely cause rocking.”

If turns and altitude changes are gradual, there’s little rocking. After going a short distance along the northern coastline, I made a wide turn and returned directly above the shipyard while viewing the roadside below.

“Now, I’ll begin descent.”

I landed it back on its foundation. It would be fine on the sea too, but we had other tasks like installing the sonic cannon later.

The ship came to a stop. After a moment of silence, King Melvin smiled and said:

“Hmm… I told you I wanted something that would become the foundation for future airships, and you splendidly met my expectations. Theodore, Alfred, this is magnificent. Well done.”

“Your words are too generous.”

Both Alfred and I bowed.

We plan to build more airships. As a symbol of friendship between Verdugal and Silvatoria, one sister ship each. Furthermore, we intend to design vessels suited for purposes like transport ships.

“Elliot. You’ll be heading to your wedding aboard the Sirius, correct? I’m sending Stephania as my representative, so you should reassure the baron’s retainers.”

“Yes! I deeply thank Your Majesty for your gracious consideration.”

“As proof that Sir Elliot has indeed built friendship with the Kingdom of Verdugal in Silvatoria, I shall accompany you as well,” said Princess Adriana with a smile.

With this… I suppose we’ve completed everything we needed to do before departing for the Barony of Silun. Once we load minimal food and water, we’ll depart for the Barony of Silun as scheduled.

“The other day you said the cabins were narrow… but this is a splendid room.”

Then, on the day we set off for the Barony of Silun. When I guided Princess Stephania and Princess Adriana to their cabin, the two looked around the room and smiled.

“As it’s the VIP suite, we tried to do everything we could. Please note that chairs, desks, and such are all fixed in place. For safety when moving around the ship, it might be best to use Levitation just in case.”

There were several large cabins like this. To increase capacity, there were also smaller cabins with just bunk beds, a desk, and luggage space for four people… but we couldn’t possibly put the two princesses there.

Well, if we have enough crew members to spare, we don’t hesitate to open up the larger rooms too. For this journey, we have quite a few companions… but well, we should be able to assign everyone to the larger rooms alone.

The lineup for the trip to the Barony of Silun included, first, our Party Members. The wedding couple themselves, Elliot and Camilla. Then VIPs like Princess Stephania and Princess Adriana, plus members from the Demon-Slaying Knight Order like Mercedes and Elmer who would serve as the princesses’ escorts.

The reason escorts were selected from the Demon-Slaying Knight Order was partly because it was the wedding of their Commander Elliot, representing the members.

Then, as it’s the maiden voyage, Alfred and his group who worked on the ship, and Old Sigmund and his workshop members. For performing at the wedding, Justia, Dominique, and Cyrille also offered their cooperation.

“A wedding, huh. I’m looking forward to it. I quite like those,” said Tephra’s figure.

Tephra, who had returned to her mountain, also appeared in Termwills, and upon learning of Elliot’s wedding, she said she wanted to go to bless them, so she joined us abruptly. A wedding receiving blessings from the Moon Goddess and a High Spirit… Well. Whether you call it spiritually potent or something else…

Well, regardless of the special nature of the attendees, it’s quite a large group.

With so many people, we needed to explain the ship’s facilities and structure to prevent confusion. I guided them through various facilities like the kitchen and toilets.

“Can we go out on the deck while the ship is flying?”

“We’ve embedded magic tools in the bow to manipulate wind and deploy a barrier… so you can go out on the deck even during flight. But considering sudden turns, it’s better not to go out except during low-speed flight. If we seem to have time to spare later, I’ll reduce speed to create time for deck access.”

“That would be lovely.”

“The view from an airship is exceptional, after all.”

Princess Stephania and Princess Adriana looked at each other and laughed. It was good to see them enjoying themselves.

After finishing the explanations… we finally departed for the Barony of Silun. Once we changed to stable flight toward the Barony of Silun, I had Old Sigmund take over piloting.

Old Sigmund and Valentina had moved the ship several times during test flights, so they could pilot without issues.

Those with magical knowledge or aptitude like Ashley, Claudia, Marlene, Rosemary, Elliot, and Elmer could also pilot. Well, with the caveat that we’re not traveling at maximum speed.

Anyway, Old Sigmund’s piloting skills were reliable, so I moved to the round table area at the front of the bridge to relax.

Each chair had cylindrical drink holders on the armrests where wooden cups could be placed. The bridge was also equipped with a carbonated drink server… but for now, tea was poured.

“Finally, huh.”

“Yeah. We’ve been busy lately, but maybe we can take it easy until arrival.”

I returned the smile Grace gave me.

“Brother Elliot’s wedding… I want it to be wonderful,” said Ashley.

Perhaps she was organizing the arrangements in her head, as she made Magic Circles appear and disappear in her hand.

“Kennel-san and I have coordinated too, so I’m sure it’ll go well.”

When I said this to reassure Ashley, she nodded with a calm expression.

We also plan to use the airship and magic for some wedding production. Well… we’ve built up know-how at the theater, so there shouldn’t be any problems.

“I think it’ll be quite shocking for the Barony of Silun’s residents, though.”

Rosemary covered her mouth with her feather fan, shaking her shoulders in amusement. Sheila nodded emphatically too, while Irmhild gave a wry smile. Marlene was beaming.

Marlene had been holding Harvesta to prevent the pot from breaking during takeoff due to shaking… but Eclair and Balor were perched on the chair backs, making it unusually lively.

Seraphina seemed—interested in the crystal panel monitors, peeking at the pilot’s station from behind.

As for Claudia, she was giving a wry smile at Rosemary’s words, but then she seemed to notice something and pointed to a corner of the bridge.

“Is that… that Guardian?”

“…Yeah. It seems to appear sometimes.”

Near Lavigne’s dedicated seat, a golden wolf figure had appeared unnoticed. Whether it had substance or not was unclear—its outline was mist-like and indistinct… but it was unmistakably a wolf silhouette.

…It was just wandering around the ship normally, but moreover, it seemed able to go outside the ship too. Lionel from the Demon-Slaying Knight Order said he saw it walking around the shipyard’s plaza. I don’t know how far it can separate, though.

It didn’t seem hostile, and I haven’t heard of anyone being threatened or attacked by it. It kept a subtle distance from Lavigne too, but there didn’t seem to be any mutual threatening.

“A Spirit, huh. I think Theodore’s assessment is correct.”

When the golden wolf met Claudia’s gaze, it quietly bowed its head. Probably showing respect as the Labyrinth’s master, I suppose. If it’s cooperating with us, that’s undoubtedly reassuring.

Well, setting the golden wolf aside… first, let’s focus on Elliot and Camilla’s wedding. I need to do my part to make it lively too.

+++

# **332 – Dance of Flowers and Light**

The Sirius flew toward the Barony of Silun as the highway stretched out below them.

The new propulsion method was quite stable. With minimal ship sway, reduced consumption, and the ability to maintain a brisk speed, they would likely reach the Barony of Silun in no time.

“We have some time to spare, so shall we reduce our speed until arrival?”

“Oh? We’re already that close?”

“Since we’re channeling the wind resistance from forward movement into rear propulsion… it’s certainly more efficient than using sails.”

“Hmm. Impressive work.”

Charlotte analyzed the Sirius while Old Sigmund lowered his hand over the crystal sphere, reducing the ship’s propulsion. As propulsion decreased, so did the lift generated by the main wings. In its place, the Levitation Furnace activated to support the ship, and the passing scenery slowed to a leisurely pace.

“We’ll be traveling at low speed for a while. You may go out on the deck, but please don’t forget to bring your Magic Tool if you cannot use Levitation.”

The announcement echoed through the speaking tubes to all parts of the ship.

“Why don’t you go out on the deck too? You must be curious about how it looks while sailing, no?”

“Indeed. May I leave the bridge to you then?”

“Hmm. No problem. Magical Power consumption is low anyway.”

Well then, I’ll leave Caduceus on the bridge just in case. He can detect and handle any abnormalities immediately.

And so we all went out on the deck for a bit.

Marlene chased after Eclair and Balor at a trot, heading toward the middle of the deck. She had been looking after Harvesta for a while, but now Claudia seemed to be taking care of her. Claudia smiled when she saw Marlene.

“I thought the wind would be strong, but it’s not bad at all.”

Princess Stephania showed a bright smile. The deck was protected from wind, making it surprisingly quiet for being in flight.

“We’ve created a wind Barrier. It also helps reduce resistance.”

Rosemary explained to Princess Stephania.

“So you’re shaping it to minimize wind resistance and channeling it backward?”

“That’s right.”

“I see. So you’re optimizing efficiency even in such details.”

Princess Stephania and Princess Adriana nodded in admiration.

“It’s good that it’s clear. Perfect wedding weather with lovely sunshine.”

Grace smiled.

“Mmm… indeed.”

The sunlight was warm. The highway leading to the Barony of Silun looked peaceful.

“Be careful.”

“Yes.”

Slightly later, Elliot emerged through the opened door. He was holding Camilla’s hand, escorting her.

“Are you here to see the view too, Elliot-san?”

“Yes. I remember the scenery around here. Camilla suggested we come see it directly rather than through the Crystal Panel.”

Saying this, Elliot gazed at the landscape below from the deck railing, narrowing his eyes.

“That mountain shape, that river… how nostalgic… I never imagined I’d be returning like this from the sky to marry Camilla. It feels a bit unreal.”

As Elliot looked into the distance, Camilla shook her head.

“No. Welcome home, Elliot.”

Exchanging these words, Elliot and Camilla drew close together. Ashley watched them with a gentle smile.

Eventually—the Barony of Silun came into view. Since Old Sigmund didn’t know details like the location of the Silun family estate, he returned to the pilot’s seat and steered the ship toward the mansion.

The Crystal Panel showed the astonished faces of the Barony of Silun’s residents.

Some looked up from the streets. Others peered out from windows.

Men and women, young and old, residents, soldiers, adventurers—all sorts of people emerged from their homes, pointing at the ship.

However, Kennel had previously informed them about the airship’s arrival. There was no major confusion. Still, the residents seemed stunned at first… but soon they began jumping up and down, waving their hands, and raising cheers to show their welcome.

The barony was already in a celebratory mood. Nearly everyone was dressed up, the streets overflowed with floral decorations, and the atmosphere was vibrant.

From the deck, Ashley, Princess Stephania, and Princess Adriana waved, and the residents and adventurers waved back with bright smiles… creating quite a lively scene.

That said, flying over residential areas felt oppressive. We maintained a moderate distance, detouring at a leisurely pace as we headed toward the Silun family estate.

Behind the Silun estate was a small grove. According to Ashley, that land also belonged to the baronial family and was used by household members to gather wild vegetables and mushrooms occasionally. For parking the airship, the area above that grove seemed suitable.

Around the Silun estate, town guards were stationed for security. The lord, her brother, and his fiancée. Plus two members of the royal family visiting. Naturally, arrangements had been made to strengthen security.

“Your Highness Stephania, Your Highness Adriana, Theodore-sama—may you be in good spirits. Welcome home, Ashley-sama, Elliot-sama. Welcome to the Barony of Silun, everyone. Thank you for traveling such a long distance. I am Kennel, serving the House of Silun.”

After disembarking and heading to the estate’s main gate, we found Kennel along with the servants and retainers of the Silun family lined up before the mansion, bowing in greeting.

Father was there, as was Malcolm, who had inherited the House Broderick. Beryne from the Adventurer Guild was present too.

The plan was to proceed directly to the small temple in the Barony of Silun for the ceremony once the time came. Since announcing the wedding and arriving by airship would likely cause a festival-like commotion, we had decided with Ashley and Elliot’s group to simply embrace the excitement and let it build.

Being able to act immediately upon arrival… well, that’s thanks to having Communication Devices.

“I’ve returned, old man. Is everything prepared?”

“Yes. Everything is proceeding as planned without issue. But still… my, my, this airship is quite something.”

Kennel let out a deep breath as he looked at the Sirius.

The delicious aroma of cooking wafted from the baronial mansion, tickling our nostrils, but we wouldn’t be dining in the barony just yet. The banquet at the estate would follow the ceremony.

In this world, weddings are typically held at temples. It doesn’t matter whether it’s a temple of the Moon Goddess or the Spirit King… in any case, the process involves pledging love to each other before the Moon Goddess or Spirit King, exchanging rings, and sharing a kiss.

In this case, it would likely be held at the Moon Goddess’s temple.

“Hello, Father.”

“Hmm. It’s good to see you looking well. And… you’ve built quite the incredible thing again.”

“It wasn’t my power alone.”

When I answered, Father gave a wry smile.

“Ambassador, it’s been too long.”

Malcolm wore a gentle smile.

“Likewise, Marquis Broderick. How have you been since then? With your busy schedule, I hope you haven’t fallen ill or anything?”

“No, busy I am, but the work is fulfilling and motivating. Thanks to you, Ambassador, I’m doing well.”

Placing a hand on his chest, Malcolm bowed.

“That’s wonderful to hear.”

He seemed to have better color than when I last saw him. I hoped the stomach medicine and medicinal incense were helping maintain his health.

“To be honest, it seems today will be a magnificent ceremony. You certainly caught us off guard.”

“I’m glad you think so—it makes the effort worthwhile.”

I also exchanged greetings with Beryne from the Adventurer Guild.

“It’s been a while, Sir Theodore.”

“Likewise, Beryne-san. It’s good to see you looking well. How have the forest Monsters been since then?”

“Fufufu. With Ashley-sama’s reputation among adventurers being so favorable, things are progressing smoothly.”

Beryne let out a meaningful chuckle. It didn’t seem like mere politeness—she genuinely appeared to be doing well.

“Sir Theodore, you yourself seem to be achieving great things. My, my. A flying ship—what a surprise. And such a beautiful vessel at that.”

“Thank you.”

It seemed the airship was what caught everyone’s attention.

“Now then… Theo. I heard we’re scheduled to head to the temple ahead of you.”

“Yes. We’ll be taking carriages through the main street of the Barony of Silun just before noon, heading toward the temple.”

“I see. So the residents can see Ashley-sama, Sir Elliot, Your Highness Stephania, and Your Highness Adriana.”

“That’s right. It’s also His Majesty Melvin’s wish. He wants to reassure the barony’s residents and retainers.”

When I answered, Father nodded as if satisfied. Since King Melvin’s intentions had been communicated via the Communication Device, Father seemed to understand his purpose relatively accurately.

After brief greetings with the invited guests, as planned, Father and the others headed to the temple by carriage first.

The carriages for us and Elliot’s group—we had them moved to the designated spot to wait.

Timing it carefully, we flew in the airship to the edge of the main street within the barony.

That’s where our carriages were waiting. Several elegant black carriages stood parked.

Since they were uncovered, people could see inside from the surroundings. Or rather, that was the purpose—to show those riding to the people lining the streets.

Both Ashley and I, and everyone else, were in formal attire. Preparations were complete.

“So it’s finally time.”

Elliot, now changed into formal wear, took a deep breath. Beside him stood Camilla, clad in a wedding dress with a white veil. Camilla already seemed on the verge of tears.

“Camilla. You’re so beautiful. It suits you perfectly.”

They had kept the superstition about not seeing each other before the wedding day, so this was the first time Elliot was seeing Camilla in her wedding dress.

Seeing Camilla changed into an exquisite dress with fine decorations, Elliot smiled and spoke.

“Thank you, I’m happy…”

In response to Elliot’s words, Camilla answered with a smile that looked ready to burst into tears.

Well then—let’s begin. Standing at the edge of the deck, I expanded a Magic Circle.

A staircase made of water extended from the Sirius’s deck, winding its way to where the carriages were parked. Following the tip of the water path, glimmers of light and water bubbles performed a Wild Dance. The water staircase, bathed in sunlight, reflected light complexly, shining in rainbow colors. The residents and adventurers crowding the main street murmured at the spectacle, then raised cheers.

“This is… incredibly beautiful. Thank you, Theodore-san. I never imagined you’d go this far…”

Elliot narrowed his eyes. I returned a smile to Elliot and Camilla and answered.

“Everyone, are you ready?”

“Yeah. No problem.”

Sheila, Irmhild, Justia, Dominique, and Cyrille—the five of them played a cheerful melody, crossing the water staircase ahead of everyone else to descend to the ground.

“Then—let’s go, Camilla.”

“Yes, Elliot.”

Elliot used water-walking magic on himself and Camilla to stand on the water staircase. Camilla stepped cautiously onto the water, and the two began descending the stairs at a slow pace.

The cheers grew increasingly louder. We followed Elliot’s group at a slight distance. There were also voices praising Ashley, Princess Stephania, and Princess Adriana. Some residents threw flower petals into the air as if to bless them. Perfect. I swirled the petals upward with the wind, letting them dance around along with the bubbles and light.

We all boarded the carriages. The main couple, Elliot and Camilla, took the lead carriage. Just to be safe, I’ll have Caduceus accompany the front carriage.

Then the lord Ashley, Princess Stephania, and Princess Adriana took the next carriage.

We boarded the following carriage. Once the water staircase had served its purpose, I transformed it into a platform for Irmhild and the others, keeping it parallel to the carriages. A flying band.

Amid the smiles and cheers of the people lining the streets, escorted by the melody played by Irmhild’s group, we traveled down the main street of the Barony of Silun, heading toward the Moon Goddess’s temple.

+++

# **333 – Oath and Blessing**

Amid the cheers of the citizens lining the streets, the carriage carrying us eventually arrived at the temple.

Around Elliot’s carriage, colorful petals, bubbles, and sparkles danced before swirling upward into the sky… After a brief pause, only the petals came drifting down like a blizzard.

Simultaneously, the melody played by Irmhild and the others came to an end.

In the modest temple, the gentle-looking head priest and Head Shrine Maiden watched the spectacle with wide eyes before eventually breaking into delighted smiles. The several priests and shrine maidens lined up in the temple’s front square to welcome us reacted similarly. The barony’s retainers led by Kennel, along with Father and the other invited guests watching from inside the temple, were also smiling and applauding. Camilla’s father, Donato, wore a serene expression as well.

After disembarking from the carriage, Elliot and Camilla were guided deeper into the temple by shrine maidens, while we joined the line of invited guests.

“First… allow me to express our joy at safely reaching this blessed day. And welcome back. It is wonderful to have you return to us, Elliot-sama.”

The head priest greeted Elliot and Camilla with words of blessing.

“Thank you. I too am delighted to have returned to my homeland together with Lady Ashley and Camilla. I am deeply grateful to have received such warm congratulations from so many people. To all present here today, I offer my deepest thanks and appreciation once more.”

“It feels as if I’m dreaming. I cannot express enough gratitude for being able to experience this day and for receiving such warm blessings from so many people.”

“The Lady Shuas must have been watching over your feelings for Elliot-sama, Camilla-sama. This is truly a joyous occasion.”

In response to the Head Shrine Maiden’s words, Camilla bowed quietly. Even if Elliot hadn’t returned, she would have continued waiting for him, so the citizens’ enthusiastic blessings were understandable.

“Moreover, we hear that even the High Spirit Tephra-sama has come all the way from Silvatoria to offer her blessings. It’s like something from a fairy tale or play—an exceedingly rare occurrence—but combined with Lady Shuas’s blessing, she will surely watch over you both.”

The temple had been informed that Tephra would be coming to offer her blessings. As the Head Shrine Maiden spoke, everyone’s gaze turned to Tephra, who responded with a cheerful smile.

“Indeed. I heard that a dear one of my ally Theodore was getting married. The warm atmosphere filling this land is good. Truly good.”

Her frankness was something unimaginable from the title of High Spirit. The head priest and Head Shrine Maiden’s expressions relaxed at Tephra’s good humor, breaking into smiles. And to think the goddess Shuas herself was also present. The actual person, Claudia, simply sat with a gentle smile, remaining quiet.

“Now then, you two, please step before Lady Shuas.”

As Elliot and Camilla approached the statue of Shuas, the shrine maidens made gestures of prayer. They were offering prayers to the goddess Shuas, asking her to bless the couple’s future. A radiance of the goddess’s blessing enveloped Elliot and Camilla.

“Elliot-sama, please make your vow of love before the goddess Shuas-sama and the Spirit Tephra-sama.”

“I, Elliot Rodias Silun, vow before the goddess Shuas and the Spirit Tephra to take Camilla Elgrim as my wife and love her for all my life.”

“Camilla-sama, please make your vow of love before the goddess Shuas-sama and the Spirit Tephra-sama.”

“I, Camilla Elgrim, vow before the goddess Shuas and the Spirit Tephra to take Elliot Rodias Silun as my husband and love him for all my life.”

At their words, the head priest and Head Shrine Maiden nodded with satisfaction. Each time they finished their vows, the blessing’s radiance enveloping them grew more powerful.

“Now, exchange your vow rings.”

Elliot to Camilla. Camilla to Elliot. Each took the other’s hand and slipped on a ring. They were matching Mithril Silver rings. The settings held vivid blue gems… perhaps sapphires?

“Now then, the vow kiss.”

Elliot lifted the veil, meeting Camilla’s tear-moistened eyes.

Then—their faces slowly drew closer, they closed their eyes, and quietly exchanged a kiss. The blessing’s radiance reached its peak, spreading explosively throughout the entire temple as they kissed. The rings they wore now seemed to have gained some magical power from this, emitting a faint, hazy glow that wasn’t merely light reflection.

Cheers and thunderous applause erupted from the attendees. Kennel was dabbing his eyes with a handkerchief, and Ashley was also applauding with teary eyes.

The smiling head priest waited for the applause to subside before solemnly speaking.

“At this very moment, blessed by both goddess and spirit, a new couple has been born here. Once more, let us have your warm applause!”

Another round of loud applause erupted. Then the wedding ceremony moved on to congratulatory speeches from the attendees. First was from the lord, Ashley.

Ashley stepped before everyone, picked up the hem of her skirt to curtsy, then raised her head confidently with a smile as she delivered her speech.

“Elliot brother-sama, Camilla sister-in-law-sama, congratulations on your marriage. I am truly delighted that we have safely reached this celebratory day. I am also proud of everyone’s efforts that made this day possible. From me as well, I offer my thanks once more.”

Ashley smiled toward Kennel. Kennel responded with tearful gratitude. Then Ashley quietly closed her eyes. After one or two breaths, she opened them and spoke.

“Thinking back… I imagine both Elliot brother-sama and Camilla sister-in-law-sama endured great hardships to reach this day. However, your story of overcoming those hardships will surely give courage to many citizens and provide vitality for tomorrow. I believe Father-sama and Mother-sama would be truly happy. Really… congratulations.”

Loud applause erupted from everyone. Yes. With content acknowledging the efforts of the prepared retainers and mentioning the citizens, it made for a good speech from a lord, didn’t it? The word “hardships” could apply to various aspects of the barony and baronial family too.

“Accordingly… we have decided to provide food and drink for the citizens in the square, so please make the announcement.”

“Yes! Understood, Ashley-sama!”

As Ashley spoke with a smile, a guard saluted cheerfully and ran off to deliver the message. It wasn’t exactly all-you-can-drink-and-eat, but as a gesture of gratitude from the baronial family, it would further boost the celebratory mood. Those who wanted more drinks or food would have to pay out of their own pockets, but surely the citizens’ and adventurers’ purse strings would loosen today. It would undoubtedly be a day-long festival.

Next, Princess Stephania stepped forward, curtsied gracefully, and delivered her speech.

“I have come as a representative of my father, His Majesty Melvin. Congratulations on your marriage this time. I offer my felicitations to the House of Silun.”

Then Princess Stephania mentioned Elliot’s future.

“Sir Elliot, despite suffering injuries in a ship accident and losing his memory, made a name for himself in Silvatoria’s renowned Magic Knight Order—and has now returned to Verdgar like this. His martial prowess and courage. The connections he built in Silvatoria and his sincere character—my father spoke very highly of them.”

“Such undeserved praise.”

“Going forward, we expect that martial prowess to serve him well as Commander of the Demon-Slaying Knight Order, and that character to greatly contribute to friendship with Silvatoria. My father also mentioned eventually wanting to entrust him with a northern region.”

An “Ooh…” of astonishment escaped from the retainers. For Princess Stephania, who had prefaced her remarks as representing King Melvin before such a crowd, to state this so explicitly—it was equivalent to King Melvin’s guarantee. Though they were congratulatory words, the mention of future matters meant… the baronial family’s retainers wouldn’t have to worry about various concerns anymore. Since the territory would be distant, there would be little conflict of interest with Ashley either.

The baton of speeches passed to Princess Adriana. Princess Adriana also curtsied before speaking with a smile, her voice ringing clearly.

“I am Adriana, entrusted with fostering friendship with your nation as a representative of my father, King Eberhart. This was truly a wonderful wedding ceremony. I offer my congratulations to you both. As Her Highness Stephania said, Silvatoria looks forward to Sir Elliot’s future achievements. Please become a bridge of friendship between our nation and yours.”

And this was the final confirmation from Princess Adriana. With both Verdgar and Silvatoria sides speaking, it increased the credibility and certainty of the matter.

Conversely… objecting to this decision would mean having complaints about the intentions of both King Melvin and King Eberhart. Well… no objections would likely come from anywhere.

“Such excessive consideration for a junior like myself. I am truly grateful. Though lacking in talent, I will devote my full efforts.”

Elliot returned a bow, and loud applause erupted. Elliot waited for it to subside before speaking again.

“And—I would like to express my gratitude to the Otherworld Ambassador, Sir Theodore, who made such a wonderful ceremony possible. Without Sir Theodore, I would not be here today. To His Majesty Melvin and His Majesty Eberhart. I intend to strive diligently so that I may repay the great debt I owe Sir Theodore.”

“Thank you. Congratulations on your marriage. I look forward to our continued association from now on.”

Elliot’s words also referred to recovering his memories. Though he couldn’t speak too much about it… it concerned both Ashley and the Demon-Slaying Knight Order. I answered with those two meanings in mind. Another round of loud applause and cheers arose from the attendees.

Yes. Regarding the Barony of Silun… there should be no more worries now. The applause and cheers continued on and on, seemingly without end.

+++

# **334 – Feast and Renaming**

“Congratulations, Camilla.”

“Thank you, Father.”

Camilla, with tears in her eyes, and Donato, with a gentle smile, exchanged words.

“My congratulations on this occasion.”

Kennel, who had been watching them, quietly bowed his head and offered words of blessing. Though Kennel also wore a quiet smile, his eyes were red.

“Kennel-dono… I can finally rest easy too. What do you say? Shall we drink through the night?”

“No, no, that would be too much. I have other plans later, and more importantly, I can’t keep up with Donato-dono’s drinking prowess. But if I have some free time, I’ll join you for a few drinks.”

“That’s more like it.”

So… after the ceremony, we were scheduled to ride the carriage again and hold a banquet at the Silun Baron’s residence. I’ll get off the carriage temporarily and head to retrieve the Sirius.

When I boarded the Sirius, a golden wolf was positioned in front of the pilot’s seat. I had left Ignis on watch on the deck too… but it seems he wanted to keep watch himself as well.

As I approached, the golden wolf slowly stood up, moved as if to yield the pilot’s seat, and twisted the corner of its mouth.

…Hmm. Well then, I suppose I’ll move the ship. I should park it above the grove, just like when we arrived in the Barony of Silun.

While gazing at the Barony of Silun, which had already turned into a festive uproar, I moved above the grove and parked the ship. Since I have a meeting later that will also serve as entertainment for the banquet, I plan to bring Harvesta along to the Silun Baron’s residence. I’ll also bring the Monster Pumpkin I brought from Termwills. As I used Levitation to float the pumpkin and prepared to disembark, the golden wolf also came out onto the deck.

“Are you coming to the banquet too?”

When I asked, the golden wolf shook its head. I suppose it intends to keep watch over the airship like this. Well, it’s not a shipyard. If it’s going to protect the ship, that’s certainly appreciated.

“Well… it should be fine. Ignis is standing by too, and without knowing how it works, no one can operate it. You should come along.”

When I said that, the golden wolf hesitated slightly before nodding.

After all, the power source is the golden wolf’s main body, and it has an elusive nature, so if it comes to it, I should be able to cut off the energy supply, right?

“Still… it’s inconvenient to keep calling you ‘you’.”

If I were to give it a name, it would probably be Sirius, but that would conflict with the ship’s name. As I muttered these thoughts, the golden wolf stared intently at me.

…Does that mean it wouldn’t mind me giving it a name?

“…How about Alpha?”

It’s a name taken from alpha wolf, indicating the leader of the pack, and from Alpha Canis Majoris.

The golden wolf didn’t say anything in particular, simply sitting regally on the deck. I can’t really tell if it likes it or not, but it doesn’t seem to be protesting. Its tail slowly swayed largely from right to left.

Well… I suppose Alpha is acceptable.

So I left the ship in Ignis’s care and descended from the deck to the grove with Alpha, Harvesta, and the Monster Pumpkin.

“Whoa. I arrived first, it seems.”

Though I reached Ashley’s mansion, the carriage hadn’t arrived yet. Checking through my visual link with Caduceus, it seemed they had just passed through the main street and would be here soon.

Hmm. The Monster Pumpkin takes up space. I’ll tell the servants first and have them place it somewhere out of the way.

And just as everyone arrived at the mansion, the banquet began. Irmhild and the others continued to volunteer as musicians, playing bright and cheerful music. With five people acting as musicians, they said they would take turns eating and manage well.

Since there were many family members, it seemed they had opened up the great hall of the Silun Baron’s residence, arranged tables and chairs there, and prepared an environment where people could freely talk with each other.

Alpha was drawing attention just like Tephra, but it was well-behaved. It was sitting quietly on the floor with Lavigne. Alpha was also having its head petted by Marlene and Charlotte.

It seems to have something like a physical form.

“Theodore-sama, Ashley-sama. Congratulations on this occasion.”

“Yes, thank you.”

The baron’s retainers came to greet us one after another. Since we’re the lord and his fiancée, we should properly fulfill our roles here. Given that the Silun Baron’s family’s future looks bright, there don’t seem to be any people trying particularly hard to sell themselves. They seem to be strictly following etiquette and trying not to dampen today’s celebratory mood.

The Silun Baron’s family has had various hardships. With former garrison captain Oslo causing a scandal, they’re probably straightening their collars.

“To meet Elliot-sama again… and on such a happy day at that… sob”

Since greetings were coming to me too, it’s only natural for today’s main characters, Elliot and Camilla.

They seemed quite busy, receiving congratulatory words and greetings in turn from the Silun Baron’s family’s retainers and servants. Some retainers were crying as they greeted Elliot.

Princess Stephania and Princess Adriana also seemed to be receiving greetings in turn. Mercedes and Elmer, who were surrounding the two princesses, also seemed tense.

“Good work, both of you.”

And—just as the round of greetings finally settled down and things calmed, Grace smiled wryly.

“Can we finally settle down and eat some food?”

I also returned a wry smile.

Since Kennel had been preparing for several days, the well-stewed dishes were exquisite. The meat seemed to melt the moment it entered your mouth.

“Delicious.”

Sheila said while bringing stew to her mouth. It seemed the performance team would take turns eating, starting with Sheila.

“The town was like a huge festival.”

“Yes. I could see it from the Sirius too, but it was quite lively.”

I nodded at Ashley’s words. It was like a drink and sing revelry. Everyone was dressed up, dancing and singing in the streets. Ever since we arrived on the Sirius, our efforts to liven things up with the show seem to have paid off.

“By the way, I’ve issued notices for the adventurers to gather at the Guild and drink there. Even if they get drunk, the likelihood of trouble occurring with the residents should be low.”

Beryne said with a smile. Indeed, I saw adventurers raising mugs filled with ale in front of the Adventurer Guild, toasting.

As always, Beryne is flawless, you could say. It’s probably consideration tailored to the Barony of Silun.

“Speaking of which… is that Evil Weed the Harvesta-kun you mentioned?”

Noticing Harvesta placed on the window frame behind me, Beryne asked. She probably heard some of the circumstances from Kennel.

“That’s right. Ashley grew it with Water Magic from when it was a seed.”

“So the monster’s properties are determined by the environmental magical power during its childhood. Of course, there are differences depending on the species, and there are inherently violent species too.”

Beryne nodded at Claudia’s words.

“…That story is quite interesting.”

For the Adventurer Guild, if it’s a story related to monster properties, they probably can’t let it pass.

Hmm. If we’re going to talk about Harvesta, it might be better to mention it before everyone gets too deep into their drinks. I’ll also call Father and Malcolm and discuss it with them.

“—So, this is the pumpkin in question.”

When I brought the Monster Pumpkin into the great hall using Levitation, cheers of “Oh!” rose up. Between Harvesta being held quietly by Ashley and the giant pumpkin, they were quite eye-catching. They might be excellent at livening up the banquet.

Since the baron’s retainers are entrusted with managing villages throughout the territory, well, it’s probably appropriate to talk about it in this place.

“Even though it grew that big, doesn’t the taste worsen?”

“I cooked and ate it, and it was sweet and delicious.”

“I’ve also been planting the Evil Weeds I received along with crops behind the mansion, and they’ve grown quite large too.”

Said Kennel. It seems the Evil Weed farming method is progressing smoothly at Ashley’s mansion as well.

“Since we have the opportunity, shall we cook this pumpkin here and serve it?”

“That sounds interesting.”

“Then, shall we cut it up?”

“Shall I do it? If you keep it floating with Levitation, I can cut it up.”

Rosemary asked. …Hmm. It would probably look better than my Water Magic cutting. I’ll leave this to Rosemary.

When I nodded, a Magic Circle expanded at the tip of Rosemary’s feather fan. Then, as she flashed the feather fan two or three times, the Monster Pumpkin was severed by Magic Thread.

“Today is a celebration, so we have to liven things up.”

Rosemary hid her mouth with her feather fan and laughed quietly. The servants collected the floating pumpkin pieces and carried them to the kitchen. The guests seemed to be enjoying themselves, which was most important.

“As for future challenges… I want to investigate whether the soil’s strength will be depleted when planting the next crop after producing such large crops. What happens when Evil Weeds go through generational changes. And then… other crops… particularly what happens when used with wheat.”

“Hmm. A truly interesting story.”

“Indeed. Wheat probably won’t grow larger, but if it helps crop growth, the harvest might stabilize.”

For Father and Malcolm, of course, and for the barony’s retainers too, this isn’t someone else’s problem. They were nodding with serious expressions.

“If small crops grow larger, that alone would reduce suffering from hunger. If there’s surplus, livestock would fatten too. There still seem to be things to investigate… This might be a tremendous discovery.”

Father was groaning with a serious expression. Does that mean we can expect increased production of livestock products as a secondary effect? That’s certainly true. Dairy cows would produce more, and farm horses would have more strength.

“So… I’d like to recruit farmers to experimentally plant the nature-changed Evil Weeds and grow wheat. If continuous cropping issues arise, I’ll restore the land’s fertility with Water Magic and Earth Magic, and even if it doesn’t work out, I’ll provide compensation for cooperating with the experiment. It’s also something His Majesty Melvin is supporting.”

“A wonderful story. There are people interested in this topic, so I’ll convey what you just said to them too. They’re scheduled to visit the mansion tomorrow.”

It seems Kennel has been properly laying the groundwork. With Kennel’s selection, there probably won’t be any mistakes.

“But if that’s the case… I feel calling them Evil Weeds etc. is somewhat inappropriate.”

“Hmm. If their nature has changed, shouldn’t we change the name too? Harvesta was the name Ashley-sama gave to the individual, right?”

The barony’s retainers exchanged words. Then their gazes gathered on me.

…Hmm. Renaming Evil Weeds.

“…How about Noble Leaf? I get the feeling they see us more as partners than protectors.”

Considering the nature of wild Evil Weeds, it might be because of their solitary nature. Helping the growth of surrounding plants might also fit the word ‘noble.’

This story about Harvesta and Evil Weeds—now Noble Leaf—is also positive news for the Barony of Silun. Among the banquet attendees, happy smiles were noticeably prominent.

+++

# **335 – The Magician's Grandson**

Elliot’s return, his marriage to Camilla, and their future. With bright topics like the Noble Leaf piling up and Irmhild and the others’ performance layered on top, the banquet had become quite lively.

“The barony’s future is secure, isn’t it?”

“Indeed, completely so.”

From the perspective of the Silun barony’s retainers, that’s exactly how things appeared.

The retainers seemed to be happily getting drunk, chatting and laughing as the festivities continued, but as dusk fell, they returned to inns throughout the town, and the banquet came to a close. Those staying at Ashley’s residence would be the people who came on the Sirius, Father, Malcolm, and Donato, who had promised to share drinks with Kennel.

“Speaking of which… I have something I’d like to communicate to the Moon Temple in the territory—”

With fewer people around, I informed Father, Malcolm, and Kennel about the communication method using the Moon Temple shrine maidens’ prayers and the teleportation using the temple.

“Hmm. So you’re saying the Moon Temple shrine maidens’ prayers reach Termwills?”

Father asked back after hearing my explanation. I’ve become quite accustomed to explaining this part—it’s a new spell formula of the Moon Temple, a technique that can be used by Claudia, an important figure at the Moon Temple.

“That’s correct. This means we can respond quickly if demons or others appear.”

Though I can contact Father and Kennel through communication devices.

Even for the demon group that’s probably aiming for their leader’s revival, the catalyst to cross the barrier seems to be quite precious… They don’t appear to have much spare capacity or time to attack places other than Termwills, but this is just a precaution.

“Understood. I’ll take note.”

Father nodded, and Kennel and Malcolm also nodded with solemn expressions due to the involvement of demons. Next, I need to take Claudia to the Moon Temples in Gartner County and the Marquisate of Broderick… That shouldn’t be a problem.

With the banquet over, I was shown to the room where I’d be staying tonight. It was quite spacious. The sense of the furniture and furnishings was also good—probably the taste of the previous Baron Silun or Kennel.

“Please make yourself comfortable. When the bath is ready, a servant will come to fetch you. If you need anything, please don’t hesitate to ask.”

“Thank you. Ah, I’d like to confirm tomorrow’s schedule.”

I asked Kennel.

“Before noon, someone who wants to cooperate with the Noble Leaf experiment is scheduled to arrive.”

“Understood.”

Hmm. Since the Sirius is fast, it seems we’ll have some time to relax in the barony.

Whether it counts as a honeymoon or not, Elliot and Camilla will be staying in the Silun barony for several days.

Thinking that having too many people around might make it hard to relax, our plan is to stay one night in the Silun barony, then take Father and Malcolm on the Sirius to extend our trip to Gartner County and the Marquisate of Broderick, and on our way back pick up Elliot and Camilla to return to Termwills.

This relates to what I discussed with Father earlier, but we also have the purpose of increasing the locations where Claudia can teleport. Old Siegmund and Valentina also have business in Gartner County, like visiting Mother’s house and paying respects at her grave.

I sat down in a chair and tilted my teacup.

“Speaking of which… Is the temple in the Silun barony really that small in scale?”

When I asked this, Claudia nodded.

“That’s right. The temple’s scale is somewhat small, so it’s not suitable for teleportation.”

“In that case, creating a monument seems like the best approach.”

When I came to Ashley’s residence before, I created a hidden room underground—it would probably be best to create a monument there. Well, monuments do have some disadvantages though.

Claudia thought for a moment before raising her head and speaking.

“That’s right. Using applications of barrier magic and contract magic, we could make it so only the ruler of this land can use it… That should work, don’t you think?”

“You mean like in Lady Tephra’s and Marquis Zilbolt’s territories?”

“Yes. By covering the monument installation area with a barrier and making it inaccessible to anyone except Ashley and her companions, we should be able to prevent misuse of the monument.”

I see. Ashley will eventually rule the barony, and she’ll inevitably travel between Termwills and the barony more frequently. If there’s a way to move other than Claudia’s teleportation magic, that would be even better.

We decided it would be better to do it today rather than carry the work over to tomorrow, so we proceeded to install the monument immediately.

We moved from Ashley’s room to the underground hidden room. We created a hidden passage in one corner of the hidden room, with stairs leading down and a small room, where we would install the monument.

“Well then, let’s begin.”

Claudia raised her hand in the center of the second basement’s small room, and green sparkles gathered before her eyes. Just as an especially strong radiance appeared, the same monument we see in the labyrinth was enshrined there. Then a magic circle spread from Claudia’s feet.

“Ashley, your blood. One drop is enough.”

“Yes, Claudia-sama.”

Ashley took a knife, made a small cut on her fingertip, and let a drop of blood fall on the small room’s floor. From there, a strong light ran to the four corners of the room—and a barrier was born.

This would make it possible to travel between the monument in my house’s basement and the one in Ashley’s house’s basement. To use monuments within the labyrinth, you need to reach that location… So as long as we don’t invite others here, the number of people who can use this monument to travel will be extremely limited. This should minimize the disadvantages as much as possible.

“Ashley. Your hand.”

“Yes.”

I took Ashley’s hand and used healing magic on the small cut on her fingertip. The healing magic I can use only has first-aid level effectiveness, but it’s enough to close this level of cut. After confirming that Ashley’s wound had closed, I asked.

“Does it hurt?”

“I’m fine. Thank you, Theodore-sama.”

Ashley covered her hand with her other hand and smiled.

—The next day. Elliot and Camilla met at the breakfast table… They were already showing affection from the morning, with Elliot pulling out Camilla’s chair for her.

Those two have always gotten along well, so there don’t seem to be any particular problems. If their marital relationship is going smoothly, that’s all that matters.

After finishing breakfast and relaxing for a while, a visitor came to Ashley’s residence. It was a resident of the Silun barony who wanted to cooperate with the Noble Leaf experiment.

Heading to the reception room with Ashley while carrying Harvesta—there was a woman with red hair in braids, wearing a robe… looking more like a magician than a farmer, waiting there.

“Nice to meet you, I’m Michelle. I’m happy to have been invited this time.”

Michelle seemed somewhat stiff. The Sirius was docked, we’d done various magical displays yesterday, and she was probably nervous about what kind of person would appear.

“Welcome. I’m Ashley Rodias Silun, the head of this house.”

“Nice to meet you. I’m Theodore Gartner.”

We introduced ourselves.

“Michelle is the granddaughter of the person who runs the magic tool shop in town. Unlike that person, she owns fields in a nearby village and researches magic and farming methods. Since she’s earned the trust of farmers in various villages, I thought she might be suitable.”

Kennel, who had shown us to the reception room, explained Michelle’s background.

I see. Someone trying to apply earth magic to farming methods. She’s definitely suitable.

…Still, I have an idea about that person running the magic tool shop in the Silun barony.

“The magic tool shop… Could it be that white-haired old man?”

“You know my grandfather?”

“Yes. When I was heading to Termwills before, I bought several magic staffs from him…”

When I answered, Michelle thought for a moment before widening her eyes.

“Ah, I remember now. Indeed, grandfather mentioned that a fine young man aspiring to learn staff martial arts came to his shop. Could that have been you, Theodore-sama?”

“…That seems to be correct. Please tell him that staff was very helpful.”

I remember talking with that shopkeeper about staff martial arts. I’m using Ouroboros now, but the practice staff I bought at that shop, while its durability was another matter, was quite comfortable to use. That must be because the shopkeeper himself practices staff martial arts.

“I think grandfather would be happy to hear that.”

Michelle showed a cheerful smile. Good. I’m glad she seems like a trustworthy person. Knowing that I’m acquainted with her grandfather seems to have eased Michelle’s stiffness.

Well, now that we’ve broken the ice a bit, let’s move on to discussing the Noble Leaf.
